<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">In this <a href="/wiki/Dutch_name" title="Dutch name">Dutch name</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">surname</a> is <i> van Dijk</i>, not <i> Dijk</i>.</div>

<p><b>Virgil van Dijk</b> (<small>Dutch pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Dutch" title="Help:IPA/Dutch">[vn dik]</a></span>; born 8 July 1991) is a Dutch professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">centre-back</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands national team</a>. Considered one of the best defenders in the world, he is known for his strength, leadership, and aerial ability.<sup id="cite_ref-Best_Defender-sportbible_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Best_Defender-sportbible-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defender-sky_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defender-sky-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He is the only defender to win <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Men%27s_Player_of_the_Year_Award" title="UEFA Men&#39;s Player of the Year Award">UEFA Men's Player of the Year</a>, and has finished runner-up for the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Football_Awards_2019#The_Best_FIFA_Men&#39;s_Player" title="The Best FIFA Football Awards 2019">Best FIFA Men's Player</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-UEFAMPOTY19_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFAMPOTY19-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After beginning his professional career with <a href="/wiki/FC_Groningen" title="FC Groningen">Groningen</a>, Van Dijk moved to <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a> in 2013, where he won the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Premiership" title="Scottish Premiership">Scottish Premiership</a> and was named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Scotland_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Scotland Team of the Year">PFA Scotland Team of the Year</a> in both of his seasons with the club, also winning the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_League_Cup" title="Scottish League Cup">Scottish League Cup</a> in the latter. In 2015, he joined <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> before signing for Liverpool in January 2018 for £75&#160;million, a <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">world-record transfer fee</a> at the time for a defender.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLiverpool_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLiverpool-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> With Liverpool, Van Dijk reached back-to-back <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> finals in <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">2018</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Champions League Final">2019</a>, winning the latter. He was also named <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Player of the Season">Premier League Player of the Season</a> in his first full season. Van Dijk later won the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2019 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>, and helped end the club's <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="2019–20 Liverpool F.C. season">30-year league title drought</a> by winning the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League" title="2019–20 Premier League">2019–20 Premier League</a>.
</p><p>Van Dijk made his international debut for the Netherlands in 2015 and became captain of his country in 2018. In 2018, he scored his first international goal in a 3–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a>. A year later, Van Dijk captained the Netherlands to the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Nations_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Nations League Final">final</a> of the inaugural <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a>, where they finished runners-up.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Van Dijk was born in <a href="/wiki/Breda" title="Breda">Breda</a> to a <a href="/wiki/Dutch_people" title="Dutch people">Dutch</a> father and a <a href="/wiki/Surinamese_people" title="Surinamese people">Surinamese</a> mother.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Growing up he would play football wherever he could – on the streets, in concrete cages, and eventually Saturday morning matches.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He combined his time playing at the <a href="/wiki/Willem_II_(football_club)" title="Willem II (football club)">Willem II</a> academy with a part-time job as a dishwasher.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc.co.uk_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.co.uk-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Having previously and unsuccessfully featured as a right-back, Van Dijk was shifted into a central defensive position in 2008, aged 17, after he grew in height by around 18 centimetres.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc.co.uk_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.co.uk-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Despite the positional shift and Van Dijk's physical growth, Willem II's reserve manager at the time <a href="/wiki/Edwin_Hermans" title="Edwin Hermans">Edwin Hermans</a> believed he had "too many limitations" which prevented him from breaking into the first team.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> In 2010, he was scouted by former Dutch international <a href="/wiki/Martin_Koeman" title="Martin Koeman">Martin Koeman</a>, who was working for <a href="/wiki/FC_Groningen" title="FC Groningen">FC Groningen</a> at the time, and he ended up completing a free transfer to the club in the same year.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc.co.uk_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.co.uk-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Groningen">Groningen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Groningen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Van Dijk initially struggled to break into Groningen's first team with club staff believing he was "overtired" after extensive playing time with Willem II's academy and reserve sides.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He made his professional debut for the club on 1 May 2011, coming on as a 72nd-minute <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> for <a href="/wiki/Petter_Andersson" title="Petter Andersson">Petter Andersson</a> during a 4–2 victory against <a href="/wiki/ADO_Den_Haag" title="ADO Den Haag">ADO Den Haag</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On 29 May, and against the same opposition, he made his first start for Groningen and scored his first professional goals, netting twice in a 5–1 win in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> play-off match.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Eredivisie" title="2011–12 Eredivisie">2011–12 Eredivisie</a> season, Van Dijk made 23 league appearances for the <a href="/wiki/Eredivisie" title="Eredivisie">Eredivisie</a> team, and scored his first regular-season goal during the club's 6–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Feyenoord" title="Feyenoord">Feyenoord</a> on 30 October 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He suffered a personal setback during the campaign, however, as soon after his 20th birthday he was admitted to hospital with <a href="/wiki/Peritonitis" title="Peritonitis">peritonitis</a> and kidney poisoning. Van Dijk later revealed that he had been close to dying as a result of the medical emergency and that the hospital had even gone so far as to ask him to sign a "sort of <a href="/wiki/Will_and_testament" title="Will and testament">will</a>" in the event of his passing.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He did, however, return to Groningen and continued to impress the following season. At the end of the campaign, and with Van Dijk having "outgrown" the club, he was offered to a number of bigger Eredivisie clubs, including <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>, all of which elected not to sign him.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Celtic">Celtic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Celtic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14_season">2013–14 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2013–14 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 21 June 2013, Van Dijk signed with <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a> for a fee of around £2.6&#160;million, on a four-year deal including a 10% selling-on fee for Groningen.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut on 17 August, replacing <a href="/wiki/Efe_Ambrose" title="Efe Ambrose">Efe Ambrose</a> for the final 13 minutes of a 2–0 <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Premiership" title="Scottish Premiership">Scottish Premiership</a> win over <a href="/wiki/Aberdeen_F.C." title="Aberdeen F.C.">Aberdeen</a> at <a href="/wiki/Pittodrie_Stadium" title="Pittodrie Stadium">Pittodrie Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he made his first start, in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Inverness_Caledonian_Thistle_F.C." title="Inverness Caledonian Thistle F.C.">Inverness Caledonian Thistle</a> at <a href="/wiki/Celtic_Park" title="Celtic Park">Celtic Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 9 November, Van Dijk scored his first Celtic goals, heading one in each half of a 4–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Ross_County_F.C." title="Ross County F.C.">Ross County</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> After a solo run, he scored the only goal of a victory over <a href="/wiki/St_Johnstone_F.C." title="St Johnstone F.C.">St Johnstone</a> on 26 December.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Dijk scored again on 26 January 2014, in a 4–0 win versus <a href="/wiki/Hibernian_F.C." title="Hibernian F.C.">Hibernian</a> for Celtic's 11th consecutive league win.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 25 February, he was sent off after 13 minutes of an eventual 2–1 loss at Aberdeen, for a professional foul on <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pawlett" title="Peter Pawlett">Peter Pawlett</a>; it was Celtic's first defeat of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> With Celtic having already won the league, Van Dijk netted again on 7 May to put his team 3–1 up away to St Johnstone, in an eventual 3–3 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He was one of three Celtic players named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Scotland_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Scotland Team of the Year">PFA Scotland Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1314PFA_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1314PFA-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Scotland_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Scotland Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Scotland Players' Player of the Year</a> award,<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> but lost out to fellow Celtic player <a href="/wiki/Kris_Commons" title="Kris Commons">Kris Commons</a><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15_season">2014–15 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2014–15 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg/170px-Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="274" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg/255px-Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg/340px-Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1278" data-file-height="2060" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Virgil_van_Dijk_2015.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Van Dijk playing for <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a> in 2015</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 July 2014, Van Dijk and <a href="/wiki/Teemu_Pukki" title="Teemu Pukki">Teemu Pukki</a> each scored twice in a 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Knattspyrnuf%C3%A9lag_Reykjav%C3%ADkur" title="Knattspyrnufélag Reykjavíkur">KR</a> in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> qualifier, putting their team into the next round 5–0 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> His first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Scottish_Premiership" title="2014–15 Scottish Premiership">Premiership season</a> came on 9 November, finishing from <a href="/wiki/Stefan_Johansen" title="Stefan Johansen">Stefan Johansen</a>'s last-minute corner for a 2–1 win at Aberdeen.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Three weeks later, Van Dijk scored the first and last goals of Celtic's 4–0 win versus <a href="/wiki/Heart_of_Midlothian_F.C." title="Heart of Midlothian F.C.">Heart of Midlothian</a> in the fourth round of the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Cup" title="Scottish Cup">Scottish Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Four days after that, his sixth goal of the season was enough for victory in a home match against <a href="/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">Glasgow</a> neighbours <a href="/wiki/Partick_Thistle_F.C." title="Partick Thistle F.C.">Partick Thistle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Dijk was again on target on 21 January 2015, opening a 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Motherwell_F.C." title="Motherwell F.C.">Motherwell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 26 February, he was sent off in the 36th minute against <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> for a foul on <a href="/wiki/Mauro_Icardi" title="Mauro Icardi">Mauro Icardi</a>, as Celtic lost 1–0 on the night, 4–3 on aggregate in the last 32 of the UEFA Europa League.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> He was again sent off on 8 March in the Cup quarter-final away to <a href="/wiki/Dundee_United_F.C." title="Dundee United F.C.">Dundee United</a> at <a href="/wiki/Tannadice_Park" title="Tannadice Park">Tannadice Park</a>, receiving a red card after eleven minutes for a confrontation with <a href="/wiki/Calum_Butcher" title="Calum Butcher">Calum Butcher</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> His suspension for the following week's <a href="/wiki/2015_Scottish_League_Cup_Final" title="2015 Scottish League Cup Final">Scottish League Cup Final</a> was overturned on appeal, as was that of <a href="/wiki/Paul_Paton" title="Paul Paton">Paul Paton</a>, who was sent off when mistaken for Butcher.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk played the full 90 minutes of the final at <a href="/wiki/Hampden_Park" title="Hampden Park">Hampden Park</a>, which Celtic won 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-2015SLC_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015SLC-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 18 March, Celtic's third consecutive match against Dundee United, Van Dijk scored in the last minute to confirm a 4–0 win in a Cup replay.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 April, Celtic contested the Cup semi-final against Inverness at Hampden, and Van Dijk opened the scoring with a free kick. After the dismissal of goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Craig_Gordon" title="Craig Gordon">Craig Gordon</a>, Celtic fell 3–2, ending their chance of a <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, again from a free kick, he confirmed a 2–1 win away to <a href="/wiki/Dundee_F.C." title="Dundee F.C.">Dundee</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> His team again won the league, and Van Dijk was included in the league's Team of the Season for the second consecutive campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-1415PFA_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1415PFA-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> He was again shortlisted for the PFA Scotland Players' Player award,<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> but lost out to another teammate, this time Stefan Johansen.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Dijk was reportedly "considering his future" in Glasgow after Celtic were knocked out of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 UEFA Champions League</a> in the qualifying rounds to <a href="/wiki/Malm%C3%B6_FF" title="Malmö FF">Malmö</a> of Sweden.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Southampton">Southampton</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Southampton">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2015–16 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 1 September 2015, Van Dijk signed a five-year contract with <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>, managed by <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Koeman" title="Ronald Koeman">Ronald Koeman</a>, for a reported £13&#160;million transfer fee.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his debut for Southampton on 12 September in a 0–0 draw against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> at <a href="/wiki/The_Hawthorns" title="The Hawthorns">The Hawthorns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sb1516_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sb1516-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, Van Dijk marked his third Premier League appearance with his first goal for the club, which came in the form of a header in the 11th minute to put Southampton in front, following a set-piece from <a href="/wiki/James_Ward-Prowse" title="James Ward-Prowse">James Ward-Prowse</a> in a 3–1 home win over <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 7 May 2016, Van Dijk signed a new six-year contract with the Saints.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2016–17 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 22 January 2017, he was named team captain of Southampton, after the departure of <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Fonte" title="José Fonte">José Fonte</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On the same day, he suffered an ankle injury against <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> This ruled him out of the <a href="/wiki/2017_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2017 EFL Cup Final">2017 EFL Cup Final</a>, which Southampton lost to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After a successful <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Southampton_F.C._season" title="2016–17 Southampton F.C. season">2016–17 season</a> at Southampton, Van Dijk was subject to interest from <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>, who apologised to Southampton for an illegal approach for the player after having reportedly made clear his interest in a move to Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 7 August 2017, Van Dijk handed in a transfer request to Southampton and released a statement along with it, emphasising his wish to join a different club in the transfer window.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Van Dijk remained with Southampton for the start of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Southampton_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Southampton F.C. season">2017–18 season</a> and made his first appearance since being injured in January, coming on as a late substitute in a 1–0 victory at <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> on 26 September.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> He made what turned out to be his final appearance for Southampton on 13 December 2017, in a 4–1 home defeat to Leicester.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> It was also his last appearance in any of Southampton's matchday squads, as he was omitted from the squad for the rest of his tenure at the club in light of speculation surrounding his future.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Liverpool">Liverpool</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Liverpool">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season_2">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0,_2018,_5_(cropped).jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="212" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0%2C_2018%2C_5_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0%2C_2018%2C_5_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0%2C_2018%2C_5_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0%2C_2018%2C_5_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1275" data-file-height="1592" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D0%B0_%D0%A4%D0%9A_%C2%AB%D0%9B%D1%96%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BF%D1%83%D0%BB%D1%8C%C2%BB_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B0_%D0%B4%D0%BE_%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%94%D0%B2%D0%B0,_2018,_5_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Van Dijk with <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> in 2018</div></div></div>
<p>On 27 December 2017, it was announced that Van Dijk would join Liverpool when the winter transfer window opened on 1 January 2018<sup id="cite_ref-pressLiverpool_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pressLiverpool-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-southamptonpress_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-southamptonpress-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> for a reported fee of £75&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLiverpool_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLiverpool-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Former club Celtic would receive 10% of Van Dijk's transfer fee, due to a sell-on clause placed in his Southampton contract.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLiverpool_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLiverpool-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Southampton claimed the undisclosed transfer fee would constitute a world record fee in football for a defender.<sup id="cite_ref-southamptonpress_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-southamptonpress-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his debut for Liverpool on 5 January in the third round of the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> and scored the winning goal with a late header in a 2–1 victory against local rivals <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> In doing so, he became the first player since <a href="/wiki/Bill_White_(footballer,_born_1877)" title="Bill White (footballer, born 1877)">Bill White</a> in 1901 to score on his debut in the <a href="/wiki/Merseyside_derby" title="Merseyside derby">Merseyside derby</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk and <a href="/wiki/Dejan_Lovren" title="Dejan Lovren">Dejan Lovren</a> built a strong partnership at the heart of Liverpool's defence, with the Dutchman being credited for improving Liverpool's previous defensive issues.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Dijk was included in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League#Squad_of_the_Season" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League Squad of the Season</a>, despite playing just half of the season in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, with the <i>UEFA Technical Observers</i> saying: "Van Dijk arrived at <a href="/wiki/Anfield" title="Anfield">Anfield</a> and provided composure and stability in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">competition's knockout stages</a>." Van Dijk played the full 90 minutes in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">2018 UEFA Champions League Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>, which Liverpool lost 1–3.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk played 22 games in all competitions in his first season with the club, scoring once.<sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2018–19 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 20 August 2018, Van Dijk was voted <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a> by <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sport" title="BBC Sport">BBC Sport</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports" title="Sky Sports">Sky Sports</a> for his performance in a 2–0 win over Crystal Palace.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk received the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Liverpool_F.C._season#Liverpool_Standard_Chartered_Player_of_the_Month_award" title="2018–19 Liverpool F.C. season">Liverpool Player of the Month</a> award for his performances in August.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 2 December, Van Dijk was awarded an assist for the winning goal in a derby match against city rivals Everton. Liverpool won 1–0 thanks to Divock Origi's 96th-minute goal, set up by a Van Dijk volley and a subsequent error from Everton goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Pickford" title="Jordan Pickford">Jordan Pickford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> The Dutchman was ultimately awarded the <a href="/wiki/Professional_Footballers%27_Association" title="Professional Footballers&#39; Association">PFA</a> Player of the Month for November 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-LFCPFA_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LFCPFA-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> On 21 December, Van Dijk scored his first goal in the Premier League for Liverpool in a 2–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> The Dutchman continued his impressive form in the 2018–19 season by winning the Premier League Player of the Month prize for December 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 February 2019, Van Dijk scored twice in a 5&#8211;0 win against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> The following month, he scored once - his first goal in the Champions League for the club - and assisted another in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>. In doing so, he became the first player since <a href="/wiki/Craig_Bellamy" title="Craig Bellamy">Craig Bellamy</a> in 2007 to score and assist a goal for Liverpool in a knock-out stage match away from home in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 April, he was one of six players nominated for the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> award alongside teammate <a href="/wiki/Sadio_Man%C3%A9" title="Sadio Mané">Sadio Mané</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he was named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> alongside Liverpool teammates, <a href="/wiki/Trent_Alexander-Arnold" title="Trent Alexander-Arnold">Trent Alexander-Arnold</a>, Mané and <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Robertson" title="Andrew Robertson">Andrew Robertson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 28 April 2019, he was named the PFA Players' Player of the Year.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_280419_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_280419-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Following Liverpool's 2–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Champions League Final">2019 UEFA Champions League Final</a> on 1 June, Van Dijk was named <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>'s man of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-MOTM_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MOTM-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Liverpool_vs._Chelsea,_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="250" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="476" data-file-height="700" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Liverpool_vs._Chelsea,_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_33_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Van Dijk playing for <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2019 UEFA Super Cup">2019 UEFA Super Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>In August 2019, Van Dijk won UEFA player of the year award. On 2 September 2019, he was shortlisted in the final three of the best FIFA football awards.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> On 23 September 2019, he was voted runner up in <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Men%27s_Player" title="The Best FIFA Men&#39;s Player">The Best FIFA Men's Player</a> and into the FIFA <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Football_Awards_2019#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="The Best FIFA Football Awards 2019">FIFpro Men's World 11</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFA2019result_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFA2019result-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIFA2019vote_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFA2019vote-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> In October 2019, Van Dijk was shortlisted as one in 30 football players for the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> At the event in December, he finished runner-up behind <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 21 December 2019, after missing the semi-final of the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup">2019 FIFA Club World Cup</a> with illness, Van Dijk played in the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Clube_de_Regatas_do_Flamengo" title="Clube de Regatas do Flamengo">Flamengo</a> with Liverpool winning the trophy for the first time in the club’s history.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFA_Final_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFA_Final-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Dijk received further recognition following the turn of the year, when he was named in the 2019 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-UTOTY2019_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UTOTY2019-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 19 January 2020, Van Dijk scored his first <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C.%E2%80%93Manchester_United_F.C._rivalry" title="Liverpool F.C.–Manchester United F.C. rivalry">North-West Derby</a> goal against Manchester United in Liverpool’s 2–0 win at Anfield in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Over the course of the 2019–20 domestic campaign, Van Dijk started and completed every minute for Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 12 September 2020, Van Dijk scored a headed goal against <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds United</a> on the opening day of the new season.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>On 17 October, he was substituted in the sixth minute of the <a href="/wiki/Merseyside_derby" title="Merseyside derby">Merseyside derby</a> after a challenge from <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Pickford" title="Jordan Pickford">Jordan Pickford</a>. On the following day, it was announced that he had suffered an <a href="/wiki/Anterior_cruciate_ligament_injury" title="Anterior cruciate ligament injury">ACL injury</a> in his right knee and would undergo surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> Van Dijk was expected to be out from six to twelve months.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> On 30 October, Van Dijk had successful surgery on his injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Van Dijk made his full international debut for <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> on 10 October 2015, in a 2–1 victory away from home against <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan_national_football_team" title="Kazakhstan national football team">Kazakhstan</a> in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> qualifier.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captaincy</a> of his country by manager Ronald Koeman on 22 March 2018,<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> and his first match as captain was a 1–0 home friendly defeat by <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> the next day.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> On 26 March, he scored his first international goal to conclude a 3–0 win over European champions <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_Gen%C3%A8ve" title="Stade de Genève">Stade de Genève</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> On 13 October, he scored in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a> champions <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> More importantly, he scored the <a href="/wiki/Equaliser_(sports)" title="Equaliser (sports)">equaliser</a> in the next match with Germany, after assistant coach Dwight Lodeweges sent him a small paper note during a break, with the request to play forward in the last minutes of the game. The goal enabled the Netherlands to win the group phase of the Nations League.<sup id="cite_ref-briefje_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-briefje-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Van Dijk is a physically strong, right-footed <a href="/wiki/Centre-back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre-back">centre-back</a>, who usually features on the left-hand side of central defence, although he can also play as a right-sided centre-back.<sup id="cite_ref-Best_Defender-sportbible_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Best_Defender-sportbible-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defender-sky_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defender-sky-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NMcG_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NMcG-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> He is gifted with pace,<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> good technique, and an eye for goal, and is an effective <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">set-piece taker</a>. Regarding his ability, former Celtic teammate Kris Commons commented that Van Dijk was "comfortable on the ball", also noting that "He had good technique and a wonderful right foot. He was good on set-pieces, some of the free-kicks he scored for Celtic are absolute wonders. He could read the game well. He had an aura about him, a confidence, because I think he knew he was good."<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neil McGuinness, senior scout at Celtic when Van Dijk was signed, called him "everything you would want if you could create a profile of the ideal central defender", praising him as a "very smooth ball-playing defender" who possesses aerial prowess, skills from dead ball situations, and "strong leadership qualities", while commenting that since his move to England, he is "more tactically aware now [...] his anticipation and timing has improved and he is a lot more of an all-rounder".<sup id="cite_ref-NMcG_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NMcG-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> McGuinness believes Van Dijk's "biggest problem" is that he "can switch off when the game is comfortable".<sup id="cite_ref-NMcG_106-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NMcG-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Steve Douglas of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Globe_and_Mail" title="The Globe and Mail">The Globe and Mail</a></i> described Van Dijk with the following words: "Powerful in the air, measured with the ball at his feet, quick, and with superb positional sense, van Dijk [<i>sic</i>] has it all."<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Dario Pergolizzi also described Van Dijk as a good marker in 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In a 2019 interview with <i><a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)">Marca</a></i>, when Lionel Messi was asked why Van Dijk was so difficult to beat, the Argentine responded: "He is a defender who knows how to judge his timing and wait for the right moment to challenge or jockey [the attacker]. He is very fast and big, but he has a lot of agility for his height. He is fast because of its [sic] great stride, and he is impressive both in defence and attack because he scores lots of goals."<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> That same year, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Merson" title="Paul Merson">Paul Merson</a> described Van Dijk as "the best in the world, and I think by a long way, as a defensive centre-half."<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sponsorship">Sponsorship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Sponsorship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Van Dijk features as the cover star of the champions edition of <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i></a> video game <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_20" title="FIFA 20">FIFA 20</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> He is endorsed by sportswear company <a href="/wiki/Nike_football" class="mw-redirect" title="Nike football">Nike</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Van Dijk commonly uses only his first name on the kit. According to his uncle Steven, this is because of a <a href="/wiki/Feud" title="Feud">family feud</a> with his father, Ron van Dijk who abandoned his wife, Virgil and his siblings during childhood.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Virgil is married to childhood sweetheart, Rike Nooitgedaght and they have a daughter, Nila.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> According to some sources in <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>, Van Dijk has <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Surinamese" title="Chinese Surinamese">Chinese</a> heritage, Hellen Fo Sieeuw, his mother, is of part-Chinese descent, the Chinese surname 'Fo Sieeuw' derives from the surname of his maternal great-grandfather, Chin Fo Sieeuw, who emigrated from <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a> to <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">Suriname</a> around 1920.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Virgil_van_Dijk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
